# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# LLVM Pass Manager Registration and Execution Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a new LLVM optimization pass is registered and executed in llvm/llvm-project. Find C++ source files that define: the PassManager template, the PassRegistry, the pass add() registration, and the pass execution order in the standard optimization pipeline (O2/O3).

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d, sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/llvm-project--a8f3c97d` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `sg-evals/gcc--96dfb333` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

As there is no\n16: /// containing IR construct for a Module, a manager for passes over modules\n17: /// forms the base case which runs its managed passes in sequence over the\n18: /// single module provided.\n19: ///\n20: /// The core IR library provides managers for running passes over\n21: /// modules and functions.\n22: ///\n23: /// * FunctionPassManager can run over a Module, runs each pass over\n24: ///   a Function.\n25: /// * ModulePassManager must be directly run, runs each pass over the Module.\n26: ///\n27: /// Note that the implementations of the pass managers use concept-based\n28: /// polymorphism as outlined in the \"Value Semantics and Concept-based\n29: /// Polymorphism\" talk (or its abbreviated sibling \"Inheritance Is The Base\n30: /// Class of Evil\") by Sean Parent:\n31: /// * https://sean-parent.stlab.cc/papers-and-presentations\n32: /// * http://www.yout

Perfect! I've successfully traced and documented the LLVM optimization pass registration and execution chain. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Key Findings:

**Files Identified (12 files):**
1. **llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManager.h** - Core PassManager template
2. **llvm/include/llvm/PassRegistry.h** - PassRegistry class
3. **llvm/lib/IR/PassRegistry.cpp** - Pass registration implementation
4. **llvm/include/llvm/PassSupport.h** - RegisterPass template
5. **llvm/include/llvm/PassInfo.h** - PassInfo metadata class
6. **llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManagerInternal.h** - PassConcept and PassModel
7. **llvm/include/llvm/IR/PassManagerImpl.h** - PassManager::run() implementation
8. **llvm/lib/IR/PassManager.cpp** - Template instantiations
9. **llvm/include/llvm/Passes/PassBuilder.h** - Pipeline builder
10. **llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilder.cpp** - Pipeline builder implementation
11. **llvm/lib/Passes/PassBuilderPipelines.cpp** - O2/O3 pipeline definitions
12. **llvm/lib/Passes/PassRegistry.def** - Pass registry macros

**The Chain:**
1. **Registration**: RegisterPass<> → PassRegistry::registerPass() stores PassInfo
2. **Pipeline Construction**: PassBuilder::buildModuleOptimizationPipeline() adds passes
3. **Encapsulation**: PassManager::addPass() wraps each pass in PassModel
4. **Execution**: PassManager::run() iterates Passes and calls through PassConcept interface
5. **Analysis Tracking**: PreservedAnalyses tracks which analyses each pass preserves

The answer has been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete details on files, symbols, and the complete execution chain.

This class is meant to be derived from by\n102: /// clients that are interested in which passes get registered and unregistered\n103: /// at runtime (which can be because of the RegisterPass constructors being run\n104: /// as the program starts up, or may be because a shared object just got\n105: /// loaded).\n106: struct PassRegistrationListener {\n107:   PassRegistrationListener() = default;\n108:   virtual ~PassRegistrationListener() = default;\n109: \n110:   /// Callback functions - These functions are invoked whenever a pass is loaded\n111:   /// or removed from the current executable.\n112:   virtual void passRegistered(const PassInfo *) {}\n113: \n114:   /// enumeratePasses - Iterate over the registered passes, calling the\n115:   /// passEnumerate callback on each PassInfo object.\n116:   LLVM_ABI void enumeratePasses();\n117: \n118:   /// passEnumerate - Callback function invoked when someone calls\n119:   /// enumeratePasses on this PassRegistrationListener object.\n120:   virtual void passEnumerate(const PassInfo *) {}\n121: };\n122: \n123: } // end namespace llvm\n124: \n125: #endif // LLVM_PASSSUPPORT_H\n126: ",
